
### CELTIC RECONQUEST of Anglo-Saxon Jarldoms ###
### DE JURE RECLAIM ###

# Jarldom of Lindsey
narrative_event = {
	id = 414101
	title = "EVTNAME414101"
	desc = "EVTDESC414101"
	major = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_castle_gate"
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	max_age = 30
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_global_flag = lindsey_created
		c_lindum = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_banovallum = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_luda = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_caistor = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_ad_abum = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c_lindum = { de_jure_liege = d_lindum }
		c_banovallum = { de_jure_liege = d_lindum }
		c_luda = { de_jure_liege = d_lindum }
		c_caistor = { de_jure_liege = d_lindum }
		c_ad_abum = { de_jure_liege = d_lindum }
		d_lindsey = { destroy_landed_title = d_lindsey }
		clr_global_flag = lindsey_created
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
		}
		name = "EVTOPTA414101"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}
		name = "EVTOPTB414101"
	}
}

# Jarldom of Pegansaete
narrative_event = {
	id = 414102
	title = "EVTNAME414102"
	desc = "EVTDESC414102"
	major = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_traveller_hills"
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	max_age = 30
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_global_flag = pegansaete_created
		c_trent_hills = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_aquae_arnemetiae = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_dovedale = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_segelocum = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_scarsdale = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = luitcoyt_renamed } }
			c_aquae_arnemetiae = { de_jure_liege = d_the_peak }
			c_dovedale = { de_jure_liege = d_the_peak }
		}
		else = {
			c_aquae_arnemetiae = { de_jure_liege = d_luitcoyt }
			c_dovedale = { de_jure_liege = d_luitcoyt }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = lerion_renamed } }
			c_trent_hills = { de_jure_liege = d_the_peak }
		}
		else = {
			c_trent_hills = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = linnius_renamed } }
			c_segelocum = { de_jure_liege = d_elmet }
			c_scarsdale = { de_jure_liege = d_elmet }
		}
		else = {
			c_segelocum = { de_jure_liege = d_lindum }
			c_scarsdale = { de_jure_liege = d_lindum }
		}
		d_mercia = { destroy_landed_title = d_mercia }
		clr_global_flag = pegansaete_created
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
		}
		name = "EVTOPTA414102"
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}
		name = "EVTOPTB414102"
	}
}

		}

	}
	
	immediate = {
		c_causennae = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		c_ad_pontem = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		c_margidunum = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		c_ratae = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		c_vernemetum = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		c_holland = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		c_bannaventa = { de_jure_liege = d_eastgwent }
		c_lactodorum = { de_jure_liege = d_eastgwent }
		c_brinavae = { de_jure_liege = d_centgwent }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = eastgwent_renamed } }
			c_gwash = { de_jure_liege = d_lerion }
		}
		else = {
			c_gwash = { de_jure_liege = d_eastgwent }
		}
		
		d_middle_angles = { destroy_landed_title = d_middle_angles }
		clr_global_flag = middleangles_created
	}

			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no

	}

# Jarldom of Wrocens√¶te
narrative_event = {
	id = 4141021
	title = "EVTNAME4141021"
	desc = "EVTDESC4141021"
	major = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_hills_woodland"
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	max_age = 30
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_global_flag = wrocensaete_created
		c_viroconium = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_deva = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}

			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}

			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_hibernicum = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_whitchurch = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c_viroconium = { de_jure_liege = d_eastpowys }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = luitcoyt_renamed } }
			c_hibernicum = { de_jure_liege = d_argoed }
			c_deva = { de_jure_liege = d_deceanglia }
			c_whitchurch = { de_jure_liege = d_eastpowys }
		}
		else = {
			c_hibernicum = { de_jure_liege = d_luitcoyt }
			c_deva = { de_jure_liege = d_luitcoyt }
			c_whitchurch = { de_jure_liege = d_luitcoyt }
		}
		if = {

			c_tegeingl = { de_jure_liege = d_deceanglia }
			c_maelor = { de_jure_liege = d_deceanglia }

		if = {

	max_age = 30
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_global_flag = hampshire_created
		c_vectis = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_clausentum = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = meonware_conquered
				NOT = { has_global_flag = meonware_destroyed }
			}
			AND = {
				c_portus_adurni = {
					is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
				}
				c_venta = {
					is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
				}
				c_vindomis = {
					is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
				}
				c_calleva = {
					is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = belgae_renamed } }
			c_vectis = { de_jure_liege = d_gradawc }
			c_clausentum = { de_jure_liege = d_gradawc }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = belgae_renamed }
			c_vectis = { de_jure_liege = d_the_belgae }
			c_clausentum = { de_jure_liege = d_the_belgae }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = meonware_conquered }
					has_global_flag = meonware_destroyed
				}
			}
			c_portus_adurni = { de_jure_liege = d_the_belgae }
			c_vindomis = { de_jure_liege = d_the_belgae }
			c_venta = { de_jure_liege = d_the_belgae }
			c_calleva = { de_jure_liege = d_eastdumnonia }
		}
		d_hampshire = { destroy_landed_title = d_hampshire }
		clr_global_flag = hampshire_created
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
		}
		name = "EVTOPTA414108"
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}
		name = "EVTOPTB414108"

# FRISIA
# High Chiefdom of Seel√¢n
narrative_event = {
	id = 414260
	title = "EVTNAME414260"
	desc = "EVTDESC414260"
	major = yes
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_rivers_landscape"
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	max_age = 30
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		c_waal = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_walacria = {
			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				c_aardenburg = {
					is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
				}
				c_wasia = {
					is_germanic_controlled_trigger = no
				}
			}
			has_global_flag = frisia_subjugated
		}
		has_global_flag = zeeland_created
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c_waal = { de_jure_liege = d_toxandria }
		c_walacria = { de_jure_liege = d_toxandria }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = frisia_subjugated } }
			c_wasia = { de_jure_liege = d_toxandria }
			c_aardenburg = { de_jure_liege = d_menapia }
		}
		
		d_zeeland = { 
			destroy_landed_title = THIS 
		}
		
		clr_global_flag = zeeland_created
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				culture = oldfrisian
				culture = frisian
			}
		}
		name = "EVTOPTA414260"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = oldfrisian
				culture = frisian
			}
		}
		name = "EVTOPTB414260"
	}
}

# High Lordship of Naoned
narrative_event = {
	id = 414423
	title = "EVTNAME414423"
	desc = "EVTDESC414423"
	major = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_castle_river"
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	max_age = 30
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		c_redon = {
			holder_scope = {
				top_liege = { 
					OR = {
						NOT = { culture_group = celtic }
						is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		c_nantes = {
			holder_scope = {
				top_liege = { 
					OR = {
						NOT = { culture_group = celtic }
						is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		c_mee = {
			holder_scope = {
				top_liege = { 
					OR = {
						NOT = { culture_group = celtic }
						is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = naoned_created
		NOT = { has_global_flag = nantes_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored } }
			d_namnetia = { de_jure_liege = k_gaul }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = roman_provinces_gaul_restored }
			d_namnetia = { de_jure_liege = k_lugdunesis_secunda }
		}
		d_namnetia = {
			set_name = ""
			adjective = ""
		}
		
		clr_global_flag = naoned_created
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA414423"
		trigger = {
			culture_group = celtic
			is_roman_ruler_trigger = no
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB414423"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { culture_group = celtic }
				is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes
			}
		}	
	}
}

# Civitas of Epidia
narrative_event = {
	id = 414543
	title = "EVTNAME414543"
	desc = "EVTDESC414543"
	major = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_lord_overlooking_bridge"
	
	only_playable = yes		
	min_age = 20
	max_age = 30
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		c_dunadd = {
			is_celtic_controlled_trigger = yes
		}
		c_cantyre = {
			is_celtic_controlled_trigger = yes
		}
		c_epidion = {
			is_celtic_controlled_trigger = yes
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = angleargyll_created }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = norse_skotsland_created }
		has_global_flag = argyll_renamed
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = norse_tyrvist_created
				has_global_flag = norse_dyrey_created
				has_global_flag = norse_skotsland_created
			}
			d_argyll = { de_jure_liege = k_south_caledonia }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = dalriada_created }
			d_argyll = { de_jure_liege = k_dalriada }
		}
		else = {
			d_argyll = { de_jure_liege = k_ulaid }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = norse_tyrvist_created 
				has_global_flag = norse_dyrey_created
			}
			d_argyll = {
				set_name = "Airer Go√≠del"
				adjective = "Argathelian"
			}
		}
		else = {
			d_argyll = {
				set_name = ""
				adjective = ""
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NAND = {
					has_global_flag = norse_tyrvist_created 
					has_global_flag = norse_dyrey_created
				}
			}
			c_scotia = { de_jure_liege = d_lorne }
			c_glen_orchy = { de_jure_liege = d_lorne }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = norse_dyrey_created } }
			c_epidion = { de_jure_liege = d_hebrides }
			c_jura = { de_jure_liege = d_hebrides }
		}
		
		clr_global_flag = argyll_renamed
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA414543"
		trigger = {
			is_roman_ruler_trigger = no
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB414543"
		trigger = {
			is_roman_ruler_trigger = yes
		}	
	}
}

			is_germanic_controlled_trigger = yes
		}
		has_global_flag = roman_chamavia
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = frisia_subjugated
				has_global_flag = saxony_subjugated
			}
			d_hamaland = { de_jure_liege = k_frisia }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = hamaland_conquered_saxon }
			d_hamaland = { de_jure_liege = k_saxony }
		}
		else = {
			d_hamaland = { de_jure_liege = k_ripuarian_franks }
		}
		
		d_hamaland = {
			set_name = ""
			adjective = ""
		}

		c_drenthe = { de_jure_liege = d_salland }
		c_twenthe = { de_jure_liege = d_salland }
		
		clr_global_flag = roman_chamavia
	}

		}

# Jarldom of Jorvik
narrative_event = {
	id = 420000
	title = "EVTNAME420000"
	desc = "EVTDESC420000"
	major = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_danes_ship_hall"
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	max_age = 30
	
	trigger = {
		is_alternate_start = no
		has_global_flag = jorvik_created
		c_eburacum = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_petuaria = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_iserium = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_cataractonium = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_delgovicia = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_dictium = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_varfedale = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_virosidum = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_cambodunum = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_legiolium = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_derventio = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_ioredale = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_danu = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_ashgill = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = deira_created }
			c_eburacum = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_petuaria = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_iserium = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_cataractonium = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_derventio = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_delgovicia = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
			c_dictium = { de_jure_liege = d_deira }
		}
		else = {
			c_eburacum = { de_jure_liege = d_ebrauc }
			c_petuaria = { de_jure_liege = d_ebrauc }
			c_derventio = { de_jure_liege = d_ebrauc }
			c_delgovicia = { de_jure_liege = d_ebrauc }
			c_dictium = { de_jure_liege = d_ebrauc }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = dunoting_renamed } }
				c_iserium = { de_jure_liege = d_ebrauc }
				c_cataractonium = { de_jure_liege = d_ebrauc }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = dunoting_renamed }
				c_iserium = { de_jure_liege = d_dunoting }
				c_cataractonium = { de_jure_liege = d_dunoting }
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = southumbria_created }

		c_dal_fiatach = { de_jure_liege = d_down }
		c_ui_blathmaic = { de_jure_liege = d_down }
		c_arda = { de_jure_liege = d_down }
		if = {
            limit = { has_global_flag = down_renamed }
            c_the_mourns = { de_jure_liege = d_down }
        }
        else = {
            c_the_mourns = { de_jure_liege = d_cuib }
        }
		
		d_port_strangford = { destroy_landed_title = d_port_strangford } 

		clr_global_flag = norse_strangford_expanded
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		name = "EVTOPTA420006"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = yes
		}
		name = "EVTOPTB420006"
	}

	only_playable = yes

		is_alternate_start = no

			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		c_kildare = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		has_global_flag = norse_wexford_expanded
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
	    c_wexford = { de_jure_liege = d_ui_dunlainge }
		c_laberus = { de_jure_liege = d_ui_dunlainge }

			c_kildare = { de_jure_liege = d_southmide }
			c_loigis = { de_jure_liege = d_southmide }
			c_regia = { de_jure_liege = d_southmide }
		}
		else = {
			c_kildare = { de_jure_liege = d_ui_ceinnselaig }
			c_regia = { de_jure_liege = d_ui_ceinnselaig }
			c_loigis = { de_jure_liege = d_ui_ceinnselaig }

			c_rath_bhile = { de_jure_liege = d_ui_ceinnselaig }

		}
		else = {
			c_rath_bhile = { de_jure_liege = d_ui_dunlainge }
			c_carlow = { de_jure_liege = d_ui_dunlainge }				
		}
		d_port_wexford = { destroy_landed_title = d_port_wexford } 

		clr_global_flag = norse_wexford_expanded
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = no
		}
		name = "EVTOPTA420006"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_norse_controlled_trigger = yes
		}
		name = "EVTOPTB420006"
	}
}
